<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:handhaven.html>handhaven</a> (8654)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hanthaven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">hanthaben</i>, itself a calque from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">maintenir</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">manūteneō</i>. Likely based also on <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:handhaven.html>handhave</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">handle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:handhaven.html>handhaven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to enforce, to maintain, to uphold</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to persevere with, to persist with/in</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remain in charge, to remain in place</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*handag</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*handugaz</i>. Corresponds to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hand</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:handje.html>handje</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klap.html>klap</a></i>.

</p>
<ol><li>gesture in which two people <a href = vnd.unilang:slap.html>slap</a> their hands</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> children's game in which players clap each other's hands</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly politics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> system of political negotiation <a href = vnd.unilang:according.html>according</a> to which compromise <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sought by exchanging policy proposals more or less wholesale on an issue-by-issue basis</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:handleiding.html>handleiding</a> (10192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">hand</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:leiding.html>leiding</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">guidance</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangar.html>hangar</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shed, <a href = vnd.unilang:hangar.html>hangar</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">hanghart</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">enclosure near a house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">hangart</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">*hamgart</i>, from Old <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*haimgard</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fence around a group of <a href = vnd.unilang:houses.html>houses</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangar.html>hangar</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangars.html>hangars</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangar.html>hangartje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:hangar.html>hangar</a>, a garage-like building for aircraft.</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:luchtvaart.html>luchtvaart</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> opslagplaats <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vliegtuigen.html>vliegtuigen</a>.</li></ol>

***hangen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a> (1250)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a merger of two distinct verbs:
</p>
<ul><li><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">haen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hān</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hanhaną</i> (transitive, strong class 7).</li>
<li><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">hangon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hangāną</i> (intransitive, weak class 3).</li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilderij.html>schilderij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hangt.html>hangt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The painting <b>hangs</b> on the wall.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:hangt.html>hangt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:schilderij.html>schilderij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b>hangs</b> the painting on the wall.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></b>

***hangmat.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangmat.html>hangmat</a> (28730)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">hamaca</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" class="extiw" title="w:Taíno language">Taíno</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tnq">*hamaka</i>, which changed to <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ham.html>ham</a>(m)ak</i> and then, <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> <i>hangmak</i>, to <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hangmat.html>hangmat</a></i>, literally “hanging mat”. Modified by influence of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hang</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mat</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. This development <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a case of popular etymology. The first attestation of such an adapted form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in a <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span></span> text; it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nevertheless believed that the German form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> indeed borrowed from Dutch. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hängematte</i> for more. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hammock</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangmat.html>hangmat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangmatten.html>hangmatten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangmatje.html>hangmatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hammock</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doek.html>doek</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uiteinden.html>uiteinden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgehangen.html>opgehangen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarin.html>waarin</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:personen.html>personen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liggen.html>liggen</a>

***hansworst.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:hansworst.html>hansworst</a> (45391)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hanswurst</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hansworst.html>hansworst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hansworsten.html>hansworsten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hansworst.html>hansworstje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> butterfingers, klutz, meathead</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> comic theatre persona, similar to a harlequin or <a href = vnd.unilang:clown.html>clown</a></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:hansworst.html>hansworst</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>

***harbinger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:harbinger.html>harbinger</a> (75500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally, a person that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sent in advance to arrange lodgings. From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">herbergeour</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">herbergeor</i> (<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">hébergeur</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*heriberga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lodging, inn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">army shelter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*harjaz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">army</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bergô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">protection</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:herbergen.html>Herberge</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">albergo</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:herberg.html>herberg</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">harbor</i>. More at here, <span class="Latn" lang="en">borrow</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:harbinger.html>harbinger</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">harbingers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A person or thing that foreshadows or foretells the coming of someone or something.
<ul><li><b>1828</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Savage_Landor" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Walter Savage Landor"><a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Savage Landor</a>, <i>Imaginary Conversations</i>, Lord <a href = vnd.unilang:brooke.html>Brooke</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Philip <a href = vnd.unilang:sidney.html>Sidney</a>
<dl><dd>I <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> by these <b>harbingers</b> who <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> coming.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> One who provides lodgings; especially, the officer of the English royal household who formerly preceded the court when travelling, to provide and prepare lodgings.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of <a href = vnd.unilang:fuller.html>Fuller</a> to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">forewarning</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">herald</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:omen.html>omen</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">premonition</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sign</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">signal</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">prophet</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:harbinger.html>harbinger</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">harbingers</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">harbingering</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">harbingered</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To announce or precede; to be a <a href = vnd.unilang:harbinger.html>harbinger</a> of.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms_2">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">herald</span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">hartnackich</i>. </p>
